Re election Announcement nMayor Angie Devanney nApril n nIt s been a trying and difficult few years n nLike many of you there were times that I struggled with so much unknown in the early days of Covid I found strength and inspiration from many places namely my family my mamas Liza Viana with her own struggles my Town hall staff I love you guys with all my heart and Father Andy Prachar who supported me in times of weakness even though I am not Catholic He coined a phrase that will forever send me right back into the memory of those early months of the global pandemic He called that feeling Leadership Tired At the end of the day we all felt the weight the heaviness of the Covid crisis plus the exposure of the wound that social and racial injustice caused all bubbling to the surface simultaneously n nMy family sacrificed While most families were reconnecting over dinner playing board games and cooking together the Devanneys were surviving off of square take out meals a day a mother and wife who spent her time on emergency management calls with the state county and local level until all hours of the day and missing a mom s stabilizing force There were high school graduations proms championship games and dance recital never held A sadness for loss of it all My husband George forged forward and ran our business without me never complaining n nI share these very personal moments because as we emerge from the Covid crisis I had uncertainty about running for re election Not because I don t love the job the hard work and the connection to this community because I most certainly do It was because my family gave selflessly so I could take care of our residents n nWe all are witnessing that Berkeley Heights is in the midst of change Many important projects cultural events and planning will shape what this community will become in the future My local county state and federal relationships my ability to get things done has kept us safe and is helping us grow Recently I had an epiphany this is not the time for a hiatus but rather a time to lean in fully after Covid derailed what we are capable of evolving into as a community n nJust a few highlights come to mind Working with Congressman Malinowki to bring to Berkeley Heights to address the aging infrastructure and drainage issues plaguing the Township Lobbying Union County to ensure the Berkeley Caterers project becomes the gateway jewel of our community providing passive recreation and walking trails along the Passaic Driving innovative ways to fund the redevelopment of Peppertown Park to be the gem of our downtown Negotiating with Fiserve to bring in in funding for the lower Columbia Park development initiative started by volunteers n nTaking care of our seniors by completing vaccine registrations Recording regular robo calls that still take place today so our older adults who may not access technology can easily stay informed Creating a senior survey to ensure that every older resident has a voice in the activities through the creation of a Senior Advisory Committee because Berkeley Heights seniors want to age in place n nRespecting our first responders at the highest level Office of Emergency Management fire and the rescue squad Appointing our new police chief who will continue the work of emphasizing community policing Bringing senior programs like the Mobile Vehicle Commission MVC to the BHPD the parking lot at town hall so our seniors don t have to travel Fighting for accreditation through our municipal insurance company to help to give our police department the tools they need Working with our Mayor s Youth Council to offer self defense training for young women n nCreating an Economic Development Committee that provided support for businesses during shut down Launching a Technical Review Committee to help starting a business in Berkeley Heights easier Passing the creation of an entertainment zone that makes Berkeley Heights a destination Pushing for improvements like green space and biking walking paths in downtown to grow the restaurant and other industries that will service the new residents moving into that area n nKeeping a mindful eye on the finances Hiring a Financial Planner to track debt pay down debt and maintain our financial health Dedicating reserves for snow sewer debt services and more Pushing to ensure redevelopment projects stay on track so that our affordable housing agreement would not be jeopardized and we can pay down the debt on the municipal complex plus permanently finance our debt n nCreating a welcoming community where everyone feels a part of Berkeley Heights Passing a permanent committee the Truth Community Healing Committee Celebrating everyone s culture through community flag raisings events Planning a multicultural street fair in the fall Assessing our diversity and inclusion in Town hall and our commissions and boards n nAdmittedly there were a few groans on Cornell Avenue when I discussed the importance to me of continuing my work in the Township But I know I have the love and support of my family to ensure I keep Berkeley Heights on the forefront n nSo it is with great pride I launch my campaign for re election We have much more to do Berkeley Heights I m looking forward to us all doing it together After all we are better together

IS OCEAN CITY BETTER OFF UNDER MAYOR JAY GILLIAN S LEADERSHIP nTHE ANSWER IS EASY n nThere s a time honored threshold question that arises in most campaigns for elected office That question is Are you better off now than you were blank years ago n nIn the case of Jay Gillian the blank is filled with a twelve marking his years of service as Mayor The question is one he welcomes and encourages all voters to ask themselves leading up to the May th Municipal Election n nLet s take a look at the conditions and situation in Ocean City today much of which is attributable to Jay s leadership working in Unity with the Community n nINFRASTRUCTURE nWhen Jay first took office the physical infrastructure of the City had deteriorated dramatically There was not even a formally adopted capital plan and hadn t been for years n nJay got to work immediately addressing the most pressing needs and developing a plan for the coming five years This capital plan has been refined and updated annually in partnership with City Council and the community n nToday twelve years later an impressive amount of the City s physical needs have been repaired improved or completely replaced Highlights of this unprecedented attention to infrastructure include paving and drainage improvements on over of the City s miles of roads and alleys improved drainage systems including for the first time huge mechanical pumping systems in several of the most flood prone areas dozens of bulkhead replacements at higher elevations than previously existed a complete replacement of the boardwalk between th and th Streets including new pavilions and restrooms beach and dune maintenance including federally funded island wide beach replenishment for the first time bayfront and lagoon dredging park and recreation improvements including a new skate park a new safe artificial turf field at Carey Stadium an expanded and refurbished Sports and Civic Center playground improvements in all four wards and several large open space purchases along th Street and in the th to th Street area n nFINANCIAL MANAGEMENT TAXES PROPERTY VALUES nOcean City enjoys strong and stable finances including the largest fund balance in City history clean audits strong bond ratings and stabile and reasonable property taxes Property values have increased on average over in the past twelve years n nEMERGENCY MANAGEMENT nDuring Jay s first term the City was severely impacted by Superstorm Sandy But we were ready The community rallied together under Mayor Gillian s leadership and was cleaned up fixed up and back in business faster than any other shore community in New Jersey Other significant hits from Mother Nature came and went in the following years and each time Ocean City did whatever was needed to protect people and property and get things back to normal n nMore recently was the world wide health emergency due to Covid Mayor Gillian didn t take any knee jerk reactions that some were calling for including a demand to close the island completely to visitors He consulted with public health professionals from the local community of medical providers and Shore Medical Center along with partners at the County Health Department and the State of New Jersey and made the tough but prudent decisions that were needed As always Jay provided for the needs of our residents setting up a system to assist those that needed help to make arrangements for their vaccinations when they became available Hundreds of people the majority seniors were helped n nQUALITY OF LIFE nDuring Mayor Gillian s tenure the City s quality of life already the envy of the region has been maintained and improved First and foremost Ocean City continues to be viewed as clean and safe by residents property owners and visitors alike It s no accident that Ocean City is always at the top of any Best of polls or lists including Best Beach Best Family Destination Best Downtown Best Boardwalk and the most tax friendly town for retirees n nMayor Gillian believes quality of life improvements go hand in hand with neighborhood improvements that attract families to live here The drainage and paving improvements in Merion Park for example were followed by significant private investment and construction of new attractive single family housing Many new young families have moved into this neighborhood It s a model that is being duplicated throughout the island n nSo ask yourself is Ocean City better off now than twelve years ago The answer s easy and a resounding yes n nAnd Ocean City is better off now and better off in the future with Jay Gillian as Mayor Vote to reelect Mayor Gillian on May th

If Environmental and Animal Extremist Groups Get Their Way What Will Our Pets Eat n nAs pet owners our dogs and cats are important to us in so many ways One of the most basic and important parts of caring for pets is feeding them Therefore it is important to consider where pet food comes from and what will happen if there is no food available to feed them That could be a real crisis if animal and environmental extremists manage to get their way and animal agriculture were to cease n nIncreased Pets Means Increased Need for Pet Food n nAccording to the American Pet Products Association pet ownership increased to about up from in The Wall Street Journal reported that pet food sales grew almost in the year ending November compared to for food overall Pets and their food are big business So how do we meet the needs of our pets n nThis is where animal proteins and products that aren t utilized by humans come in n nAnimal Byproducts in Pet Food n nPet foods use rendered animal ingredients and by products for pet food These ingredients are not only healthy but improve the sustainability of the pet food industry animal agriculture and add in valuable nutrients n nAt the American Feed Industry Association s AFIA Pet Food Conference in January of the head of food safety quality and regulatory for Pilgrims JBS USA Ansen Pond Ph D provided a detailed account of the sustainable benefits of rendering to the pet food industry n nThese benefits included significant contributions n To reduce animal protein fat and byproduct waste n Repurpose water n Reduce greenhouse gas emissions GHG n Provide fresh meat slurry ingredients to pet food processors n n nEverything But the Moo Oink and Cluck n nAnimal agriculture has a saying that they use everything but the moo or oink or cluck In the U S meals containing different meat and cuts comprise of only a portion of a livestock animal n nThe raw materials from the animals processed are recaptured and repurposed in many industries including pet food where essential amino acids and fatty acids are valuable for pet nutrition n nRoughly of raw materials from cattle from poultry and from swine are considered inedible in the U S market for human food Rather than going to waste those products are used for numerous products ranging from pet food to asphalt suture material gelatin capsules paint make up pharmaceutical products and many many more n nWater Used for Irrigation is a Valuable Byproduct of Animal Processing n nWater used for irrigation is a valuable byproduct of animal agriculture and animal processing When livestock are rendered water is removed from animal byproduct ingredients The water is collected as condensate and then renderers treat and repurpose that water for use in irrigation This equates to billion gallons billion pounds of water released back into the environment every year To put it into perspective that equates to about Mississippi Rivers n nReplacing Animal Protein and Fat Ingredients with Vegan Alternatives is Not Sustainable n nAlmost daily animal and environmental groups are pushing for fake vegan products which are simply not sustainable nor healthy The reality is this if pet food producers were to replace animal protein and fat ingredients which are by products of human food production with vegan alternatives they d have to plant and harvest an additional million acres of soybeans and million acres of corn That doesn t even take into account the additional water needed to grow those crops n nGuardian Article About Vegan Dog Food n nOn April th The Guardian published an article claiming that a peer reviewed study from the University of Winchester proves that vegan diets are healthier for dogs than commercial diets The facts are that no veterinary nutritionists advocate for vegan dog food UNLESS they are formulated by a licensed veterinary nutritionist and there are no other alternatives Cats simply cannot subsist on a vegan diet even though there are those vegans who believe they can A vegan diet for cats is inhumane causing the cat to suffer from malnutrition and a horrible death n nIt is important to note that The Guardian has received numerous grants to write against animal agriculture Therefore it comes as no surprise to find numerous flaws in the so called study and subsequent claims The researchers of the study are vegan and motivated by bias None of the researchers who participated in the study are veterinary nutritionists Most glaring is the fact that the study was funded by the food awareness organization ProVeg International n nThe study itself was based on pet owner responses It was sent to pet owners who were the only ones giving input Their pets veterinarians had no input According to the study of the dogs were fed a conventional meat diet were fed a raw meat diet and were fed a vegan diet over the period of one year nThere were no challenges given in the study either which is a basic part of scientific research The numbers vegan and raw diet are not representative of the general population Additionally the Guardian article glossed over the fact that according to the study raw fed dogs were healthier than vegan dogs n nByproducts Are NOT Bad for Pets n nAnimal byproducts are a sustainable and nutritious way to meet the needs of our pets Anthropomorphizing our pets can compromise their health according to Dr Sean Delaney a veterinary nutritionist from Davis CA Dr Delaney has gone on record as stating that dogs and cats are evolutionarily hardwired to consume the livestock leave behinds that we find disgusting feet eyes brains etc He further states that these byproducts are quite nutritious for animals Watch a cat eat a mouse and they go for the vital organs because these have the vital nutrients they need as obligate carnivores Unfortunately the ever increasing shift from agrarian to urban population has changed the way society looks at ingredients for pet food often to the detriment of the pet as in the case of imposing a vegan diet on animals that need meat to be healthy n nRegulation of Pet Food and Pet Food Safety n nPet food products are among the most highly regulated products in grocery stores Federal and state laws and regulations apply to various aspects of pet food including ingredients manufacturing processes and labeling Pet food plants are subject to inspection by the FDA and state regulators both state control officials and FDA have the authority to test pet food ingredients and the finished product n nPet food is regulated by the Food and Drug Administration FDA The Federal Food Drug and Cosmetic Act FD C Act requires that all animal foods like human foods be safe to eat produced under sanitary conditions contain no harmful substances and be truthfully labeled In addition canned food must be processed in conformance with the low acid canned food regulations to ensure it is free of viable microorganisms Title Code of Federal Regulations Part n nPet food labeling is regulated at two levels the FDA regulations require proper identification of the product net quantity statement name and place of business of the manufacturer or distributor and proper listing of all the ingredients from most to least based on weight In addition the Association of American Feed Control Officials AAFCO provide a model of regulations that states can follow n nAnimal Sourced Byproducts n nAAFCO s Model Regulations for all animal feeds require that the ingredients list include the species of animal that meat and meat byproducts come from unless the meat or meat byproducts come from cattle swine sheep or goats n nDuring the processing of animals certain parts rejected for human use can be expected to be processed into animal feed This could be meat that doesn t meet human aesthetics or internal organs Meat and meat by products from animals that have diets by other means than slaughter aren t directly suitable for animal food because they are considered adulterated They can t be used for animal feed unless they contain no chemical additives are heat treated and further processed This means that the claims by some so called pet nutritionists that dog food contains roadkill or euthanized animals is bogus disinformation n nSupply Chain Issues n nAmericans are currently experiencing what happens when there are supply chain disruptions to our food supply There are empty shelves and some basic food items simply are not available This is happening whether it is food for ourselves or food for Fluffy and Fido n nIt is easy to see how pet food is impacted Walk down the pet food aisle of grocery stores and pet food stores and you ll notice feet upon feet of empty shelves Some stores have chosen to spread out food on the shelves to make it less apparent but the fact is there s a lot of pet food missing n nCauses of Supply Chain Issues Starting in and Ongoing n nCOVID and COVID policies wreaked havoc on the world in Shutdowns and lockdowns as well as other regulations created a perfect storm of supply chain failure No sector has been left untouched from shortages of containers and trucks to move them empty containers stuck in ports and vessels waiting offshore for weeks to offload their cargo Then there were surging thefts of container cargo Once products are unloaded truck carriers are facing driver shortages and railways are overwhelmed in some areas became the year of the supply chain disruption and it s continuing into n nHow is Pet Food Impacted n nThe pet food industry mirrors the main economy Dana Brooks President of the Pet Food Institute noted recently Manufacturers are experiencing challenges in every node of the supply chain from the ingredient sourcing to transportation and employee shortages n nWhen the pandemic first started hospitality firms and other businesses linked to human food production shut down for public safety Manufacturers of pet food lost a key source of their ingredients With the vast majority of the workforce working remotely from home people turned to pets for companionship and more than million households adopted a new pet between March and December of n nEven now two years later pet food manufacturers are still facing ingredient shortages price increases in processing equipment ingredients and especially transportation Then when businesses ramped back up the pet food industry began reeling from labor shortages n nPet Food Ingredients in Short Supply n nWith pet food ingredients in short supply issues with getting aluminum for cans and added pressure are put on to deal with an already low stock of food n n nOur Pets are Important to Us n nOur pets provide companionship affection exercise and entertainment to us and we as owners want the best for them The reality is that dogs and cats belong to the order of Carnivora for a reason They need meat unless a veterinary nutritionist formulates an alternative diet for our dogs The loss of animal agriculture should animal extremists win means we either lose our pets to malnutrition or we would need to let them fend for themselves which is a death sentence too n nWe can t let that happen n nLinks to references can be found in this article on our website

would go like this n n Republicans across Missouri have demanded we use this session to address the following issues n na Election integrity reform implementing voter ID requiring paper ballots eliminating early voting and strengthening accountability for absentee voting nb Protecting women s sports nc Protecting your right to a job without losing it for not taking a COVID vaccine nd Stopping the teaching of Critical Race Theory in our schools and increasing accountability of public schools to parents ne Repealing the gas tax increase passed by moderate Republicans last year nf Opposing the Joe Biden spending spree disaster in Washington DC ng Pass a map to reinforce Republican majorities in the US Congress n nWith session days to go NOT ONE of these priorities have passed the Missouri Senate one of the reddest states in America n n As a result a minority of Republicans informally known as the Conservative Caucus are furious They have used their power in the chamber to disrupt the passage of other non priorities to try and force the moderate Republicans to bring the real and urgent issues listed above to final passage The conservatives pursued long lasting filibusters on the redistricting process fighting for a map and forced illuminating votes on other leftist leaning bills to further expose the actions of the moderate Republicans This is the heart of the contention n n In the midst of this the Republican public has become further aware of the pattern of bad votes and actions moderate Republicans have been taking This has led to a series of primary challenges to the re election of some moderate Senators in the nupcoming election cycle further heightening the tension within the Senate Chamber n n Some moderate Republicans fearing electoral backlash have begun fundraising from some very powerful special interests in Jefferson City to raise millions to defend themselves in re election notably more than million has been set aside in a special interest Political Action Committee called Right Path PAC to defend these moderates n n In addition with six open seats up for election in the Missouri Senate that brings a total of Republican seats possibly switching from the conservative side to the moderate and vice versa Already Senators are jockeying coalitions for a leadership race that will take place once the August Republican primary concludes none of the seats in question have a competitive general election n nThis is the political and policy reality of the Republican Missouri Senate right now n nAll of the contention would leave the Republican Senate Caucus if the caucus would prioritize passing the issues voters sent us here to address This isn t about social media setting differences aside listening to others or believing the person next to you is good at heart n nThis is about fighting and winning in a war of ideas happening RIGHT NOW in America that if we lose will cost the next generation of Missourians worth fighting for If that means kicking over some apple carts in Jefferson City count me in

Who is Andy Legg and why is he seeking a position on the Chambers County Public Hospital District Board I hope to answer these questions for members of our community that are not already familiar with me my family and my works within our community n nI was raised in LaPorte Texas and spent the first part of my adult life living in the Deer Park Pasadena areas In my wife Clarissa Dylan Oldest son years old at the time now and I moved to Wallisville This is the same year I became aware of the Chamber County Hospital District when I received my property tax statement in the mail Shortly after relocating we were blessed with the birth of our second Son Logan now years old and six years later our youngest daughter Cecilia aka CeCe who is now years old The decision to raise our family in the Wallisville Anahuac area is clearly one of the best Clarissa I have ever made together n nI have worked in Chambers County for over years at Covestro s Baytown site formerly Mobay Miles Bayer filling various roles in Logistics Production and most recently Maintenance Execution In my current capacity as a Contract Management Coordinator I have responsibilities for safe and efficient execution of contract maintenance on our site infrastructure This includes buildings HVAC roads ditches and utilities just to name a few I have received numerous trainings certifications while at Covestro most notably as an External Structural Fire Fighter TEEX at Texas A M University and BoardWorks Training Covestro Center for Community Engagement at Robert Morris University One of the most impactful and successful initiatives that I have been a part of was a site maintenance efficiency project where our team sought out every opportunity for money saving improvements within and outside our organization In addition to my role in maintenance at Covestro I also voluntarily serve on the sites Outreach Council Scholarship Team and also support the sites annual United Way fundraiser I was Recognized in by the United Way of Greater Baytown Area and Chambers County as Campaign Coordinator of the Year leading the sites first ever Virtual United Way Campaign during the height of the COVID pandemic n nMy volunteer work extends outside the boundaries of my Covestro family into the community where Clarissa and I raise our family I help to support the students and staff of Anahuac ISD through my participation with the Anahuac ISD Education Foundation I have been engaged with the great folks volunteering with this organization since and am privileged to have succeeded Mrs Linda Tinnerman as the foundation s President Currently on my second term as President Outside of Covestro I also support the United Way of the Greater Baytown Area and Chambers County as a member of the Community Impact Committee serving along with Kayle Smith and the United Way Grant Review Teams This year I led the Education Grant Review Team where we evaluated over in grant applications from various agencies in our surrounding communities made recommendations to our local United Way board for their approval During the COVID pandemic I also served on the United Way COVID Emergency Grant Review Team where we met on an ad hoc basis sometimes weekly to review and approve COVID related grants for agencies servicing needs within the Chamber County Area I am also a member of the Chambers County Resource Network that facilitates monthly meetings where local Non Profit organizations come together to discuss the needs within our community and look to identify resources to meet these needs n nWhat has motived me to become engaged with the Chamber County Hospital District and to seek election to one of the open at large board positions I care about people and our community Through my community engagement I have awareness of concerns for those who live in our community the tax payers and the even the folks traveling down I who are simply passing through our hospital district On a more personal note I have a child that through no action of his own has a medical condition that will likely be with him for the rest of his life Type Diabetes Additionally when I was years old this dreaded disease took someone I was very close to and I thought I d spend the rest of my life they were uninsured and in the care of a small rural hospital n nAs many of you have heard and or read there are many issues the Chamber County Hospital District is currently facing These include Timely Financial Reporting the Board needing to work harmoniously turnover in the executive management team and many more challenges that need to be overcome Together we can do this I encourage anyone to attend a monthly board meetings or to reach out to one of the board members to express your concerns I am optimistic about our future and gracious for your consideration

posted the full article below n n n nAlamo disrespecting George P Bush may kill family s political dynasty nBy Isabel Vincent nMarch am nNEW YORK POST n nAt first glance George Prescott Bush seems the ideal political candidate in a state where his family has been a powerful dynasty for decades n nThe telegenic Texas lawyer is a grandson of st US President George H W Bush and the nephew of George W Bush the rd He is the eldest son of two term Florida Gov Jeb Bush and the great grandson of US Sen Prescott Bush of Connecticut The war veteran and father of two married to blond lawyer Amanda Williams Bush is also Mexican American on his mother s side and speaks fluent Spanish n nBut that might not be enough according to critics who accuse him of being the black sheep of the family and disrespecting the Alamo Texas most treasured symbol by bringing in modern minded out of staters for its restoration n nOn Tuesday Bush and incumbent Ken Paxton beat two other Republican candidates vying to be the party s pick in the attorney general s race n nNow a critical May runoff will determine whether the fourth generation scion will be able to shore up the family s political legacy in the Lone Star State analysts say n nBut that s another problem The Bush name is not popular in Texas anymore Luke Twombly a Dallas based political consultant and former communications director of the Texas Republican Party told The Post n nPaxton the Texas attorney general since has been indicted on securities fraud charges and accused of bribery and misuse of office in a civil whistleblower lawsuit but still has the support of the state s conservatives He also has the endorsement of former President Donald Trump a situation Bush hopes to reverse by invoking Trump in his campaign ads which don t mention the titans in his own family n n Under the leadership of President Trump our country was strong and vibrant again says Bush in a campaign video At another point in the ad he notes Like President Trump I will not sit idly by while our freedoms are under attack because Texas must lead the way in fighting this radical agenda n nIf Bush is trying to capitalize on his devotion to Trump his opponents hope to end the Bush family s political dominance in Texas which began after George H W moved with his wife Barbara from Connecticut to the Lone Star State in to work in the oil business n n If conservatives unite we can end the Bush dynasty Paxton told a Lubbock radio station Wednesday The Bushes have had their chances It s time for the dynasty to end n nBush commissioner of the General Land Office in Texas has faced withering criticism from both Democrats and fellow Republicans for his work restoring the Alamo historic site He s also been under scrutiny for his agency s administration of veterans homes where the COVID fatality rate was percent at seven out of nine facilities more than double the rate at the state s other nursing homes during the height of the pandemic n nIn his eagerness to seek endorsements from Trump Bush has broken with members of his own family becoming the black sheep of a clan that has little patience for Trump s hold on the Republican Party n n I can t imagine that George P is getting a lot of love from his family in pursuit of the Trump endorsement said Twombly n nAlthough he likely needs Trump s endorsement to win the race others say Bush lacks the same leadership genes that propelled his relatives to political victory n n Well maybe he s not exactly a black sheep but Bush is not the guy Jerry Patterson Bush s predecessor on the General Land Office told The Post I knew and and Bush is not a guy who is a leader He s a decent enough fellow but if you want someone to make hard decisions he s out of it He avoids controversy puts his head down n nAs commissioner of the GLO he has played fast and loose with the Alamo the state s most sacred historic site he added Patterson was so incensed with what he called Bush s lack of transparency and bungling of the monument s restoration that he decided to run against him to get his old job back in n nWhen Patterson lost to Bush in the Republican primary for the commissioner s job he decided to back Bush s Democratic opponent Miguel Suazo in the commissioner s race He wasn t the only one n n Never in my memory have all primary opponents of a Republican candidate either endorsed the primary winner s Democratic opponent or stated publicly they wouldn t vote for the Republican primary winner Patterson said n nIn addition to Patterson losing Republican primary opponents in the race Rick Range Davey Edward and David Watts all refused to back Bush n n There are things that are more important than your party said Patterson who ran the GLO between and The Alamo is Texas n nAmong the criticisms of Bush s work on the restoration of the site which will include a new museum with a rooftop garden is a lack of transparency and the hiring of a Philadelphia design firm that suggested incorporating modern glass walls n n Calling in all these out of state so called experts who knew nothing about the Alamo nothing about what it means to Texas was Bush s first mistake according to Range a retired firefighter in an interview with the Texas Monthly n n He cannot be trusted with the future of the Alamo Range told the magazine He s flip flopped more times than a catfish stranded on the bank of a river n nDespite the criticisms Bush prominently features images of the Alamo in his campaign ads which also include several references to Trump s domestic policy greatest hits n nIn his latest ad Bush reminds viewers that he is a former Navy officer deployed to Afghanistan and promises to finish Trump s wall He is filmed in dark glasses riding an all terrain vehicle in the shadow of the wall that marks the southern border with Mexico n n It s such bulls t said Patterson Every damned politician talks about the wall but the attorney general years ago I had my son Nehemiah They took me into a recovery room and where I was holding him looking at him smiling everything a new mother does with a new baby But I noticed that every time I would ask the nurse for something they wouldn t leave the room Usually nurses will just leave to go get whatever you ask for but they wouldn t leave me by myself n nEverything I asked for she would call down and have somebody else bring it up At the time I m thinking that was weird but I still never really paid attention to it n nSo the next day his doctor came in to see him and he looked at his hands and he was evaluating him and he said I think Nehemiah has Down syndrome n nI just froze n nI said Are you sure n n Yes I think he has Down syndrome but I m not for sure he said We re going to run some tests and everything when he comes to his first doctor s appointment n nSo I call my mom on the phone hysterical I was and didn t know anything about Down syndrome I got my mom on the phone and I m crying I can barely get my words out n nBut she was already waiting for my phone call My mom was taking her social work classes at the time and they had just studied Down syndrome and she already knew n nI was crying and told her that they were going to do some test at his first doctor s appointment to find out for sure I took him to that doctor s visit and that s when they confirmed that Nehemiah had Down syndrome I took that really bad to the point where they thought they were going to have somebody come pick me up at the doctor s office and drive me home but I told them that I could drive myself n nOn the way home I stopped at a gas station just bawling my eyes out sitting there in the parking lot I called my mom on the phone and I m just like Why me I m years old I have a son that has a disability I don t know anything about and I don t know what I m going to do I asked a lot of questions Why me Why him None of my friends have a kid that has a disability None of my family members None of my siblings So why me Lord Why did you choose us n nI sat there for probably about an hour talking to my mom The thing that made me start up the car and come home was when she told me You know God gives special children to special people God gave you Nehemiah for a reason You may not know what that reason is right now and you may never find out what that reason is but God gave him to you for a reason n nAfter that I started doing some research because I felt I needed a support group to learn from or talk to people who were in the same situation The closest support group was in Mount Pleasant and that was just too far away I was having a tough time because when Nehemiah was a week old I moved back home with my mother Here I was a single mother with two kids because Nehemiah and his sister are and a half months apart n nSo I was like What can I do There s nothing here for people like us The closest support group is in Mount Pleasant and that s too far to get help n nThat s when I decided to start my first Down syndrome walk I got the flyers made and everything It was mostly just my family and friends who came out Terry Camp came out and did a news story and he actually came to a few of them I wanted more parents that had kids with disabilities to show up at this walk but I had my family and my friends there who were supportive I continued to do these walks up until COVID which now I m starting back up this year n nI never would have imagined that I would give birth to a child with Down syndrome but my son is my world and if I could go back in time I would not change anything He amazes our family everyday with the things that he says and does n nNehemiah is and will always be God s special gift to me n n Shortorah Carter
